     <div class="container"> 
      <h2> Don't Panic! A developer's guide to Bitex. </h2> 
      <p> Our <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/JSON">JSON</a> <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Representational_state_transfer">REST</a> <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Application_programming_interface">API</a> lets you build applications that leverage Bitex liquidity and funding options. </p> 
      <p> Language specific wrappers and code samples can be found in our <a href="https://github.com/bitex-la">GitHub repositories</a>, we'll gladly take requests for your favourite language, but ultimately we rely on your contributions to expand our language specific catalog. </p> 
      <p> We're looking to hear from you, tell us what you need and we'll add it. We're always reachable at <a href="/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#6b030e0707042b09021f0e1345070a"><span class="__cf_email__" data-cfemail="a9c1ccc5c5c6e9cbc0ddccd187c5c8">[email&nbsp;protected]</span></a> </p> 
     </div> 
    </div>

       <div class="col-lg-9 docs-body"> 
        <h1 id="overview">Overview</h1> 
        <p> Our API endpoints support params in both application/x-www-form-urlencoded and application/json formats. </p> 
        <p> We have a sandbox environment running at <a href="https://sandbox.bitex.la">https://sandbox.bitex.la</a> you can sign up there, make dummy cash deposits and deposit bitcoins from the Bitcoin testnet. You can get sandbox coins using this <a href="http://faucet.xeno-genesis.com/">Testnet Bitcoin Faucet</a> </p> 
        <p> You should limit your use to under 5 requests a second, if you run over your usage limit you'll start getting a 429 HTTP response status. Also, beware of <a href="http://cloudflare.com">Cloudflare.com</a> which is our <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/DDoS_mitigation">DDOS mitigation</a> provider. You may find yourself being blocked by them if your IP has been blacklisted or if your usage pattern seems malicious, even when it's not. If you're being blocked by cloudflare please contact us at <a href="/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#d6beb3babab996b4bfa2b3aef8bab7"><span class="__cf_email__" data-cfemail="81e9e4ededeec1e3e8f5e4f9afede0">[email&nbsp;protected]</span></a> and we'll review your case and whitelist your IP accordingly. </p> 
        <br> 
        <hr> 
        <h1 id="use-cases">Example Use Cases</h1> 
        <p> Our API is the result of working hand in hand with developers of real world, business critical applications. These are just some examples of what developers are building, we can't wait to see what you'll do with it. We want to expose as much functionality as possible, but at the same time we want to get out of your way and make things simple for you, please contact us at <a href="/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#6f070a0303002f0d061b0a1741030e"><span class="__cf_email__" data-cfemail="98f0fdf4f4f7d8faf1ecfde0b6f4f9">[email&nbsp;protected]</span></a> with suggestions on how to make your life easier. </p> 
        <br> 
        <br> 
        <div class="docs-box" id="market-watch"> 
         <h2 class="docs-box-header">Market Watch</h2> 
         <div class="docs-box-body"> 
          <p> A good example of a Market Watch is <a href="http://bitcoinaverage.com">bitcoinaverage.com,</a> it's a website providing real-time price and trade volume data about several bitcoin exchanges, and Bitex is one of them. </p> 
          <p> They get our market summary from the <a href="#ticker">Ticker</a> endpoint. </p> 
          <p> If you're building something similar you may also have a look at our <a href="#order-book">Orderbook</a> for market depth and <a href="#transactions">Transactions</a> for last hour traded volume, or even better, the <a href="#last-24-hours">Last 24 Hours</a> of aggregated data in a format that is friendly for <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Candlestick_chart">candlestick graphs.</a> </p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="docs-box" id="trading-arbitrage"> 
         <h2 class="docs-box-header">Trading and Arbitrage</h2> 
         <div class="docs-box-body"> 
          <p> Before you start trading or arbitraging Bitcoin you should get a full view of the current market and your position using the <a href="#transactions">Transactions</a> endpoint to learn about the most recent volatility, <a href="#order-book">Orderbook</a> to get the current market depth and <a href="#profile">Profile &amp; Balances</a> to check your BTC and USD available balances. </p> 
          <p> Once that's done it's easy to place <a href="#create-bid">Bids</a> and <a href="#create-asks">Asks</a> in Bitex, as well as following their execution status in your <a href="#orders">Active Order List</a> </p> 
          <p> Or you can check your recent <a href="#user-trades">Individual Trades.</a> to see what got bought and/or sold. </p> 
          <p> We have an open source robot that can be used as an example of our API usage, and can also be used to do arbitrage between Bitex and other exchanges <a href="https://github.com/bitex-la/bitex-bot" target="_blank">Fork it on github.</a> </p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="docs-box" id="accept-payments"> 
         <h2 class="docs-box-header">Accept Bitcoin Payments</h2> 
         <div class="docs-box-body"> 
          <p> You can start accepting bitcoin payments using our <a href="#payments-overview">Payments Endpoint</a> </p> 
          <p> We can quote your customer local currency into bitcoin so you can request them to pay <em>"100 EUR in Bitcoin".</em> </p> 
          <p> Once you receive the Bitcoin we can convert it to USD at the best BTC/USD bitex price, or keep it as Bitcoin if you want to. </p> 
          <p> We even give you your own Web Point of Sale where customers can create a new Payment to you in a self-service way, or pay for an existing one you created via API. </p> 
          <p> All funds will be credited to your bitex account and from there you can proceed to request a withdrawal <a href="#create-coin-withdrawal">to your own Bitcoin wallet</a> or <a href="#create-cash-withdrawal">to your bank account.</a> </p> 
          <p> All exchange rates used for quoting come from our <a href="#rates">Rates API.</a> </p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="docs-box" id="remittances"> 
         <h2 class="docs-box-header">Remittances</h2> 
         <div class="docs-box-body"> 
          <p> Remittance workflows with bitcoin usually require exchanges to take either one of two roles: <br> 1) Turning fiat into bitcoin at the sender's request and then forwarding the produced bitcoin to another exchange which will... <br> 2) Sell the bitcoin for fiat and then process a withdrawal on the receiving party's behalf. </p> 
          <p> Bitex can take any of those roles, provided the sender or receiver has an account and an accepted KYC Profile in Bitex. </p> 
          <p> Our <a href="#resellers">Reseller API</a> lets you create new accounts in Bitex and you can then use the <a href="#kyc-profiles">KYC Profile</a> endpoints to produce a valid profile. </p> 
          <p> For sending a remmittance your can instruct the person to <a href="#create-cash-deposit">Deposit Fiat</a> into their Bitex balance using one of the supported mechanisms, <a href="#create-bid">Buy Bitcoin</a> in the BTC/USD orderbook and then <a href="#create-coin-withdrawal">Withdraw Bitcoin</a> to the desired bitcoin address. </p> 
          <p> For receiving a remmitance you can use our <a href="#payments-overview">Payments API</a> to get a fresh bitcoin address to receive the money to and automatically convert it from BTC to USD at the best market price in Bitex, then request a <a href="#create-cash-withdrawal">USD Withdrawal</a> to their bank account, or whatever other withdrawal method is supported by Bitex in the customer's country. </p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="docs-box" id="asset-management"> 
         <h2 class="docs-box-header">Asset Management</h2> 
         <div class="docs-box-body"> 
          <p> Our best example in this area is Koibanx, which is a company managing investment funds, receiving USD from their customers to be invested in Bitcoin. </p> 
          <p> They use our <a href="#resellers">Reseller API</a> to create and manage accounts for their customers, thus leveraging Bitex <a href="#kyc-profiles">KYC and AML,</a> and safe Bitcoin vault. </p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <br> 
        <hr> 
        <h1 id="api-keys">Your API keys</h1> 
        <p> You authenticate to the Bitex API by provinding one of your API keys as a POST or GET parameter called api_key. You can have several active API keys at once. </p> 
        <p> It's your responsibility to keep all your API keys safe. Always use the https protocol when making your requests. Revoke your API keys immediately if you think they're compromised. </p> 
        <div class="api-keys-region"></div> 
        <div class="login-for-api-keys-region"></div> 
        <div class="complete-kyc-for-api-keys-region"></div> 
        <br> 
        <hr> 
        <h1 id="market-data">Public Market Data</h1> 
        <p> Our public market data endpoints let anyone check our market's volume, prices and transaction history. It also provides aggregateted candlestick-like data points for the last 24 hours, 7 days and 30 days of trading. </p> 
        <p> You don't need an API key (or even sign up to Bitex) to access the public market data. </p> 
        <br> 
        <br> 
        <div class="docs-box" id="api_ticker"> 
         <h2> <strong>Ticker</strong> </h2> 
         <div class="docs-box-body"> 
          <p> Overview of current market prices and trade volume, including <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Volume-weighted_average_price">Volume-Weighted Average Price.</a> </p> 
          <strong>URL</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <span class="method">GET</span> 
           <span class="url">https://bitex.la/api-v1/rest/<em>btc_usd/market/ticker</em></span> 
          </div> 
          <strong>JSON Response</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <span><pre class="highlight"><code><span class="p">{</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"last"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mf">1230.0</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Last transaction price</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"price_before_last"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mf">1220.0</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Helps you tell if price is going up or down.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"open"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mf">1198.45875559</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// What the price was 24 hours ago.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"high"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mf">1230.0</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Highest price for the past 24 hours.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"low"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mf">1193.2507548</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Lowest price for the past 24 hours.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"vwap"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mf">1208.57944642</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Volume-Weighted Average Price for the past 24 hours.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"volume"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mf">16.45315074</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Transacted volume for the last 24 hours.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"bid"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mf">1226.5583985</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Highest current buy order.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"ask"</span><span class="p">}</span><span class="w"> </span></code></pre> </span> 
          </div> 
          <strong>cURL example pastebox</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <textarea class="pastebox" rows="1">curl -X GET https://bitex.la/api-v1/rest/btc_usd/market/ticker</textarea> 
          </div>

          </div>

           <span><pre class="highlight"><code><span class="p">{</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Bids are sorted, best paying bids come first.         <div class="docs-box" id="api_transactions_archive"> 
         <h2> <strong>Transactions Archive</strong> </h2> 
         <div class="docs-box-body"> 
          <p> Returns a JSON list of lists representing all individual trades that took place since Bitex started trading until the beginning of the current hour, sorted by descending date. </p> 
          <p> This may be a large download so keep in mind we may not let you retrieve it more than a few times per hour. Don't worry though, it only changes once an hour. </p> 
          <strong>URL</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <span class="method">GET</span> 
           <span class="url">https://bitex.la/api-v1/rest/<em>btc_usd/market/transactions_archive</em></span> 
          </div> 
          <strong>JSON Response</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <span><pre class="highlight"><code><span class="p">[</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">[</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">1492795215</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// UNIX timestamp.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">80310</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Transaction ID.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mf">1243.51657154</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Price Paid.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mf">4.60321971</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Amount Sold.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">]</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">]</span><span class="w"> </span></code></pre> </span> 
          </div> 
          <strong>cURL example pastebox</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <textarea class="pastebox" rows="1">curl -X GET https://bitex.la/api-v1/rest/btc_usd/market/transactions_archive</textarea> 
          </div> 
         </div>

        <h1 id="rates">Exchange Rates</h1> 
        <p> Our exchange and funding rates API helps you get the most accurate price estimates when transfering money between services and performing currency exchanges. </p> 
        <p> As Bitex provides several cash in and cash out options through several third party providers, and each of those charges their own fees and may offer a different exchange rate from and to local currencies, you will find it useful to understand all the steps involved in each funding/withdrawal and buy/sell operation. </p> 
        <p> We offer a tree structure where you can lookup the steps for going from one currency to another as follows: <br> from_what/from_where/what_to/where_to/method </p> 
        <p> For example, if you have United States Dollars in the bank and you want to use them to fund your Bitex account via an international wire transfer, you can look up the conversion in the JSON tree as follows: tree.usd.bank.usd.bitex.swift </p> 
        <p> You can also explore the full tree through our own <a href="/calc">Calculator.</a> </p> 
        <p> Some of the provided strategies are for reference only and are not tied to any particular service, for example: usd/cash/vef/cash/reference </p> 
        <div class="docs-box" id="api_rates_tree"> 
         <h2> <strong>Rates Tree</strong> </h2> 
         <div class="docs-box-body"> 
          <p> Retrieves the full exchange rates tree, we suggest you explore it in your favorite REPL console, or alternatively check which paths are available using our <a href="Calculator">/calc</a> </p> 
          <strong>URL</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <span class="method">GET</span> 
           <span class="url">https://bitex.la/api-v1/rest/<em>rates/tree</em></span> 
          </div> 
          <strong>cURL example pastebox</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <textarea class="pastebox" rows="1">curl -X GET https://bitex.la/api-v1/rest/rates/tree</textarea> 
          </div> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="docs-box" id="api_using_the_tree"> 
         <h2> <strong>Using the tree</strong> </h2> 
         <div class="docs-box-body"> 
          <p> Each conversion strategy is a list of operations to be applied to the original amount in the original currency, once all operations have been applied, you'll get the resulting amount expressed in the destination currency. </p> 
          <p> Operations are a list of single steps, each one with it's own type representing a currency exchange for a given rate, a fixed or percentual fee to be substracted, or a minimum fee scheme where a percentage is charged unless it's lower than the minimum. </p> 
          <strong>JS Example</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <span><pre class="highlight"><code><span class="kd">function</span> <span class="nx">calculate</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="nx">original_amount</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="nx">operations</span><span class="p">){</span>
  <span class="kd">var</span> <span class="nx">result</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="nx">original_amount</span><span class="p">;</span>
  <span class="k">for</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="kd">var</span> <span class="nx">i</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">;</span> <span class="nx">i</span> <span class="o">&lt;</span> <span class="nx">operations</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">length</span><span class="p">;</span> <span class="nx">i</span><span class="o">++</span><span class="p">){</span>
    <span class="kd">var</span> <span class="nx">step</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="nx">operations</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="nx">i</span><span class="p">];</span>
    <span class="k">switch</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="nx">step</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">type</span><span class="p">){</span>
      <span class="k">case</span> <span class="s1">'exchange'</span><span class="err">:</span>
        <span class="c1">// Apply a currency exchange for the given rate.</span>
        <span class="nx">result</span> <span class="o">*=</span> <span class="nx">step</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">rate</span><span class="p">;</span>
        <span class="k">break</span><span class="p">;</span>
      <span class="k">case</span> <span class="s1">'percentual_fee'</span><span class="err">:</span>
        <span class="c1">// Substract the given percentage.</span>
        <span class="nx">result</span> <span class="o">-=</span> <span class="nx">result</span> <span class="o">*</span> <span class="nx">step</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">percentage</span> <span class="o">/</span> <span class="mf">100.0</span><span class="p">;</span>
        <span class="k">break</span><span class="p">;</span>
      <span class="k">case</span> <span class="s1">'fixed_fee'</span><span class="err">:</span>
        <span class="c1">// Substract a fixed amount.</span>
        <span class="nx">result</span> <span class="o">*=</span> <span class="nx">step</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">amount</span><span class="p">;</span>
        <span class="k">break</span><span class="p">;</span>
      <span class="k">case</span> <span class="s1">'minimum_fee'</span><span class="err">:</span>
        <span class="c1">// Either substract a percentage or a fixed amount, whichever is higher.</span>
        <span class="kd">var</span> <span class="nx">fixed</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="nx">step</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">minimum</span><span class="p">;</span>
        <span class="kd">var</span> <span class="nx">percentual</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="nx">result</span> <span class="o">*</span> <span class="nx">step</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">percentage</span> <span class="o">/</span> <span class="mi">100</span><span class="p">;</span>
        <span class="nx">result</span> <span class="o">-=</span> <span class="nx">fixed</span> <span class="o">&gt;</span> <span class="nx">percentual</span> <span class="p">?</span> <span class="nx">fixed</span> <span class="p">:</span> <span class="nx">percentual</span><span class="p">;</span>
        <span class="k">break</span><span class="p">;</span>
    <span class="p">}</span>
  <span class="p">}</span>
  <span class="k">return</span> <span class="nx">result</span><span class="p">;</span>
<span class="p">}</span>

<span class="c1">// Estimate how much bitcoin can be obtained by</span>
<span class="c1">// sending 1000 USD to bitex via international wire.</span>
<span class="kd">var</span> <span class="nx">tree</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="p">...;</span> <span class="c1">// The full tree with all possible conversions.</span>
<span class="nx">calculate</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="mi">1000</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="nx">tree</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">usd</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">bank</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">btc</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">bitex</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">swift</span><span class="p">);</span>
</code></pre> </span> 
          </div> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="docs-box" id="api_hosted_calculator"> 
         <h2> <strong>Hosted Calculator</strong> </h2> 
         <div class="docs-box-body"> 
          <p> For convenience, we also offer a calculator endpoint which receives an initial amount and the path to the desired conversion. </p> 
          <strong>URL</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <span class="method">GET</span> 
           <span class="url">https://bitex.la/api-v1/rest/<em>rates/calculate_path</em></span> 
          </div> 
          <strong>JSON Request</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <span><pre class="highlight"><code><span class="p">{</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"amount"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">1000</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// The amount to convert from.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"path"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"usd/bank/btc/bitex/swift"</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Path to calculator to use.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">}</span><span class="w"> </span></code></pre> </span> 
          </div> 
          <strong>cURL example pastebox</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <textarea class="pastebox" rows="4">curl -X GET https://bitex.la/api-v1/rest/rates/calculate_path -H "Content-Type: application/json" -d '{
  "amount": 1000,
  "path": "usd/bank/btc/bitex/swift"
}'
</textarea> 
          </div> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <hr> 
        <h1 id="account-information">Account Information</h1> 
        <p> These endpoints give you access general information about your account such as your balances, movements including deposits, withdrawals as well as executed bids and asks, and your list of KYC Profiles, a collection of all the people or legal entities associated to your bitex account in any capacity. </p> 
        <p> If you're looking for your individual trades see <a href="#user-trades">Your latest Trades.</a> </p> 
        <p> Most accounts only need one KYC Profile, if you need to create sub-accounts have a look at our <a href="#resellers">Reseller API.</a> </p> 
        <div class="docs-box" id="api_profile_and_balances"> 
         <h2> <strong>Profile and Balances</strong> </h2> 
         <div class="docs-box-body"> 
          <p> Returns a JSON object with aggregated information about your account. </p> 
          <strong>URL</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <span class="method">GET</span> 
           <span class="url">https://bitex.la/api-v1/rest/<em>private/profile</em></span> 
          </div> 
          <strong>JSON Request</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <span><pre class="highlight"><code><span class="p">{</span><span class="nt">"api_key"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"your_api_key"</span><span class="p">}</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Your bitex.la API key</span><span class="w"> </span></code></pre> </span> 
          </div> 
          <strong>JSON Response</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <span><pre class="highlight"><code><span class="p">{</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"usd_balance"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mf">10000.00</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Total USD balance.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"usd_reserved"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mf">2000.00</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// USD reserved in open orders.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"usd_available"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mf">8000.00</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// USD available for trading.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"btc_balance"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mf">20.00000000</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Total BTC balance.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"btc_reserved"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mf">5.00000000</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// BTC reserved in open orders.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"btc_available"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mf">15.00000000</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// BTC available for trading.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"fee"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mf">0.5</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Your trading fee (0.5 means 0.5%).</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"btc_deposit_address"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"1XXXXXXXX..."</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Your BTC deposit address.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"more_mt_deposit_code"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"BITEX0000000"</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// MoreMT deposit code (deprecated).</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">}</span><span class="w"> </span></code></pre> </span> 
          </div> 
          <strong>cURL example pastebox</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <textarea class="pastebox" rows="3">curl -X GET https://bitex.la/api-v1/rest/private/profile -H "Content-Type: application/json" -d '{
  "api_key": "your_api_key"
}'
</textarea> 
          </div> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="docs-box" id="api_your_account_summary"> 
         <h2> <strong>Your Account Summary</strong> </h2> 
         <div class="docs-box-body"> 
          <p> Returns a heterogeneous JSON list of lists containing your account summary for the last 30 days, sorted by descending date. This includes Bitcoin and USD Deposits and Withdrawals as well as matched Bids and Asks (see our <a href="#api-class-reference">API class reference</a> ). </p> 
          <strong>URL</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <span class="method">GET</span> 
           <span class="url">https://bitex.la/api-v1/rest/<em>private/account_summary</em></span> 
          </div> 
          <strong>JSON Request</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <span><pre class="highlight"><code><span class="p">{</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"api_key"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"your_api_key"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Optional. If present, the endpoint will show</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// your full account summary, instead of just the last 30 days.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Please do not abuse this endpoint in full history mode. </span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"full"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="kc">true</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">}</span><span class="w"> </span></code></pre> </span> 
          </div> 
          <strong>JSON Response</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <span><pre class="highlight"><code><span class="p">[</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">[</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// 1 means it's a Bid, see our API class reference.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">12345678</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Bid's unique ID</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">946685400</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Creation time as UNIX timestamp</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Orderbook (1 is BTC/USD)</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mf">100.00000000</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Amount you wanted to spend initially.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mf">10.00000000</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Remaining Amount to be spent.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mf">1000.00000000</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Price: Maximum price you're willing to pay per unit.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// An integer representing the order status:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// 1 - Received, queued to check if you have enough funds.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// 2 - Active and being executed.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// 3 - To be cancelled as soon as possible.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// 4 - Cancelled, no further executed. We do not know the recipient of this withdrawal.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"UY"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Country ouf destination for this withdrawal. Possible values are AR, BR, CL, CO, PE, UY, MX and US.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"UYU"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Currency in which this withdrawal will be paid, Possible values are ARS, BRL, CLP, COP, PEN, UYU, MXN and USD. Check our rates API for cash_out currency conversion rates.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"bb"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Cash Out method, one of:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// "international_bank" International bank transfer.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// "bb" Other payment method, to be arranged with our staff.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"Billy Bob"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// An optional custom label for this withdrawal info</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Kyc Profile ID for which this deposit was instructed.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">{</span><span class="c1">...</span><span class="p">},</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// The Withdrawal Instructions provided for this withdrawal.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">3</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Id of the actual currency debited on bitex, as you may end up receiving local currency from a withdrawal to your USD balance. 3 means you'll be debited United States Dollars. We may enable balances in other currencies in the future.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">]</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">]</span><span class="w"> </span></code></pre> </span> 
          </div>

           <textarea class="pastebox" rows="4">curl -X GET https://bitex.la/api-v1/rest/private/account_summary -H "Content-Type: application/json" -d '{

  "full": true
}'

        <h1 id="api_kyc_profiles_overview">KYC Profiles Overview</h1> 
        <p> KYC Profiles hold all the Know Your Customer information and documentation for the account owner or owners. </p> 
        <p> USD deposits and withdrawals can only be from and to an account belonging to one of your Bitex account registered owners. </p> 
        <p> Deposit and withdrawal limits apply to your Bitex account. New KYC Profiles that have KYC Files associated to them are temporarily accepted into the 'micro' usage tier until they are reviewed by one of our compliance officers. Having a photo ID is the minimum requirement for a KYC Profile to be accepted. </p> 
        <p> You can request a usage tier higher than micro when creating or updating a KYC Profile. All changes done to KYC Profiles will be reviewed by a compliance officer and you'll be contacted through email or phone if any further information is required. </p> 
        <p> Most accounts only need one KYC Profile, if you need to create sub-accounts have a look at our <a href="#resellers.">Reseller API</a> </p> 
        <div class="docs-box" id="api_create_a_kyc_profile"> 
         <h2> <strong>Create a KYC Profile</strong> </h2> 
         <div class="docs-box-body"> 
          <p> Create a new KYC Profile. Only usage tier presence is required, all other fields are optional and free form unless otherwise stated. We suggest you complete all of them. You want to make it easy for our compliance officers to accept your KYC Profiles. </p> 
          <p> You can create as many as you want, but you need to make sure each one created is for a real person willing to use the service. Mindless creation of KYC Profiles is considered abuse. </p> 
          <strong>URL</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <span class="method">POST</span> 
           <span class="url">https://bitex.la/api-v1/rest/<em>private/kyc_profiles</em></span> 
          </div> 
          <strong>JSON Request</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <span><pre class="highlight"><code><span class="p">{</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"api_key"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"your_api_key"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Your Bitex.la API key.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"usage_tier"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"micro"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Usage tier you want to get into one of: micro, small, medium or large.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"first_name"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"Billy"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"last_name"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"Bob"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"personal_id_number"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"33222111N"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// No particular format expected, just make sure it's a valid id number.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"personal_id_issuer_country"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"AR"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Uppercase ISO country code for the country that issued the ID</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"personal_id_type"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"passport"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Type of ID provided. It's free form but we suggest values like 'dni', 'passport', 'drivers_license'</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"tax_id"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">4333222115</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// This persons tax id (cuit for argentina)</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"birth_date"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"1970/1/30"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Year/Month/Date</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"nationality"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"brazilian"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"gender"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"male"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// We suggest male or female</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"occupation"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"Singer"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"home_address"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"Argentina, Bue..."</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Full address, including zipcode</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"work_address"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"Argentina, Bue..."</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Full address, including zipcode</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"phone_numbers"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">555120921</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"legal_entity"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="kc">true</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Boolean: Wheter they will be operating on behalf of a company # or other legal entity.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"politically_exposed_person"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="kc">true</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Boolean: Wheter they are what's considered to be politically exposed.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">}</span><span class="w"> </span></code></pre> </span> 
          </div>

officers.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">]</span><span class="w"> </span></code></pre> </span> 
          </div>

  "api_key": "your_api_key"

        <div class="docs-box" id="api_create_a_kyc_file"> 
         <h2> <strong>Create a KYC File</strong> </h2> 
         <div class="docs-box-body"> 
          <p> Create a new KYC File for a given KYC Profile, the minimal requirement for an account is a legible Photo ID. Accepted file formats are image/jpeg image/jpg image/png image/bmp image/gif application/pdf application/x-pdf </p> 
          <p class="text-warning"> This should be a multipart/form-data request. Not a regular application/json. </p> 
          <strong>URL</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <span class="method">POST</span> 
           <span class="url">https://bitex.la/api-v1/rest/<em>private/kyc_profiles/<strong>kyc_profile_id</strong>/kyc_files</em></span> 
          </div> 
          <strong>Params</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <span> api_key: your_api_key <br> document: @/home/you/Desktop/test.png <br> document_content_type: image/png </span> 
          </div> 
          <strong>JSON Response</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <span><pre class="highlight"><code><span class="p">[</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">12345678</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// KYC File id.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// KYC Profile id.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"http://.."</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Temporary URL to access this file expires in a few minutes.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"test.png"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Filename</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"image/png"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Content Type</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">10000</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// File Size in bytes</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">]</span></code></pre> </span> 
          </div> 
          <strong>cURL example pastebox</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <textarea class="pastebox" rows="4">curl https://bitex.la/api-v1/rest/private/kyc_profiles/kyc_profile_id/kyc_files \
  -F "api_key=your_api_key" \
  -F "document=@/home/you/Desktop/test.png" \
  -F "document_content_type=image/png"</textarea> 
          </div> 
         </div> 
        </div>

        <div class="docs-box" id="api_list_all_kyc_rejection_reasons"> 
         <h2> <strong>List all KYC Rejection Reasons</strong> </h2> 
         <div class="docs-box-body"> 
          <p> All possible kyc rejection reasons can be queried with this endpoint. Besides the unique code, you get detailed text in English, Spanish and Portuguese. Feel free to use the detail or show your own text based on the 'code' field. </p> 
          <strong>URL</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <span class="method">GET</span> 
           <span class="url">https://bitex.la/api-v1/rest/<em>private/kyc_rejection_reasons</em></span> 
          </div> 
          <strong>JSON Request</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <span><pre class="highlight"><code><span class="p">{</span><span class="nt">"api_key"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"your_api_key"</span><span class="p">}</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Your bitex.la API key</span><span class="w"> </span></code></pre> </span> 
          </div> 
          <strong>JSON Response</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <span><pre class="highlight"><code><span class="p">{</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"data"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">[</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">{</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"id"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="s2">"1"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"type"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="s2">"kyc_rejection_reasons"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"attributes"</span><span class="p">:{</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"detail_es"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="s2">"Algunos campos fueron inválidos"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"detail_en"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="s2">"Some fields were invalid"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"detail_pt"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="s2">"Alguns campos foram inválidos"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"code"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="s2">"invalid_fields"</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">}</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">},</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">{</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"id"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="s2">"2"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"type"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="s2">"kyc_rejection_reasons"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"attributes"</span><span class="p">:{</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"detail_es"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="s2">"La foto del documento es ilegible"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"detail_en"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="s2">"The photo ID is illegible"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"detail_pt"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="s2">"Identificação é ilegível"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"code"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="s2">"photo_id_is_illegible"</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">}</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">}</span><span class="w"> </span><span         <h1 id="trading">Trading</h1> 
        <p> Trading endpoints have everything you need to place and cancel Buy or Sell orders, as well as listing your active orders and every trade you make. </p> 
        <p> We have an open source robot that can be used as an example to our Trading API usage, and could also be used to do arbitrage between Bitex and other exchanges <a target="_blank" href="https://github.com/bitex-la/bitex-bot">Fork it on github.</a> </p> 
        <div class="docs-box" id="api_your_active_orders"> 
         <h2> <strong>Your Active Orders</strong> </h2> 
         <div class="docs-box-body"> 
          <p> Returns a JSON list of lists representing all your currently active orders, that is, orders where status is 'executing'. </p> 
          <strong>URL</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <span class="method">GET</span> 
           <span class="url">https://bitex.la/api-v1/rest/<em>private/orders</em></span> 
          </div> 
          <strong>JSON Request</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <span><pre class="highlight"><code><span class="p">{</span><span class="nt">"api_key"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"your_api_key"</span><span class="p">}</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Your bitex.la API key</span><span class="w"> </span></code></pre> </span> 
          </div> 
          <strong>JSON Response</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <span><pre class="highlight"><code><span class="p">[</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">[</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// 1 means it's a Bid, see our API class reference.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">12345678</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Bid's unique ID</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">946685400</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Creation time as UNIX timestamp</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Orderbook (1 is BTC/USD)</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mf">100.00000000</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Amount you wanted to spend initially.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mf">10.00000000</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Remaining Amount to be spent.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mf">1000.00000000</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Price: Maximum price you're willing to pay per unit.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// An integer representing the order status:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// 1 - Received, queued to check if you have enough funds.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// 2 - Active and being executed.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// 3 - To be cancelled as soon as possible.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// 4 - Cancelled, no further executed. May have some Remaining Amount.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// 5 - Completed. Fully executed, Remaining Amount should be 0.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// An integer with the cancelation reason:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// 0 - Not cancelled.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// 1 - Not enough funds to place this order.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// 2 - Cancelled per user's request.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// 3 - Other, cancelled by bitex.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mf">1.1</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Base currency amount (ie: BTC amount) produced by this Bid (so far). A sum of all the Base currency received on Buy Transactions. Fees are already deducted from this amount.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"ApiKey#1"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Bid issuer. If the order was entered via API it will be an ApiKey, if it was entered via the web UI it will be a User. May be empty for older orders.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mf">0.01</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Amount of Specie paid as fee (so far). A sum of all the fees paid on Buy Transactions.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">],</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">[</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">2</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// 2 means it's an Ask, see our API class reference.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">12345678</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Ask's unique ID</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">946685400</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Creation time as UNIX timestamp</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Orderbook (1 is BTC/USD)</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mf">100.00000000</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Amount you wanted to sell initially.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mf">10.00000000</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Remaining Amount to be sold.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mf">1000.00000000</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Price: Minimum price you're asking for each unit.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// An integer representing the order status:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// 1 - Received, queued to check if you have enough funds.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// 2 - Active and being executed.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// 3 - To be cancelled as soon as possible.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// 4 - Cancelled, no further executed.         <div class="docs-box" id="api_your_latest_trades"> 
         <h2> <strong>Your Latest Trades</strong> </h2> 
         <div class="docs-box-body"> 
          <p> Returns a heterogeneous JSON list of lists representing your most recent individual Buys and Sells for the past 7 days, with a hard limit on 500 items. This includes individual matches for any of your Bitcoin Bids and Asks. (see our API class reference). </p> 
          <strong>URL</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <span class="method">GET</span> 
           <span class="url">https://bitex.la/api-v1/rest/<em>private/trades</em></span> 
          </div>

          </div>

        <div class="docs-box" id="api_create_a_bid_buy_order"> 
         <h2> <strong>Create a Bid (Buy Order)</strong> </h2> 
         <div class="docs-box-body"> 
          <p> Places a new buy limit order spending the USD amount specified and paying the specified price or less. Returns a list representing the newly created Bid. </p> 
          <p> Bids are executed until all the USD amount is spent or until you cancel them. If someone was selling below your price you'll end up buying more than anticipated. </p> 
          <p> All Bids are accepted in the 'Received (1)' state, and are moved into the 'Executing (2)' state by our trading engine once it checks your available USD sufices to place the order, only then your Bid becomes eligible to be matched. You can check this order status in your list of <a href="#orders">Orders</a> </p> 
          <strong>URL</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <span class="method">POST</span> 
           <span class="url">https://bitex.la/api-v1/rest/<em>private/bids</em></span> 
          </div> 
          <strong>JSON Request</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <span><pre class="highlight"><code><span class="p">{</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"api_key"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"your_api_key"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">//Your Bitex.la API key.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"amount"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"10000.05"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">//Amount of USD to spend. Must be at least 1 USD.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"price"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"500.00"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">//Maximum price you're willing to pay per unit.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"orderbook"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">//Orderbook ID. Optional. Defaults to 1 which is BTC/USD</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">}</span><span class="w"> </span></code></pre> </span> 
          </div> 
          <strong>JSON Response</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <span><pre class="highlight"><code><span class="p">[</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// 1 means it's a Bid, see our API class reference.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">12345678</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Bid's unique ID</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">946685400</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Creation time as UNIX timestamp</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Orderbook (1 is BTC/USD)</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mf">100.00000000</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Amount you wanted to spend initially.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mf">10.00000000</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Remaining Amount to be spent.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mf">1000.00000000</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Price: Maximum price you're willing to pay per unit.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Always 1, meaning the order was received and queued to check if you have enough funds.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Always 0, since this order has not been cancelled.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mf">1.1</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Base currency amount (ie: BTC amount) produced by this Bid (so far). A sum of all the Base currency received on Buy Transactions. Fees are already deducted from this amount.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"ApiKey#1"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Bid issuer. If the order was entered via API it will be an ApiKey, if it was entered via the web UI it will be a User. May be empty for older orders.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mf">0.01</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Amount of Specie paid as fee (so far). A sum of all the fees paid on Buy Transactions.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">]</span><span class="w"> </span></code></pre> </span> 
          </div> 
          <strong>cURL example pastebox</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <textarea class="pastebox" rows="6">curl -X POST https://bitex.la/api-v1/rest/private/bids -H "Content-Type: application/json" -d '{
  "api_key": "your_api_key",
  "amount": "10000.05",
  "price": "500.00",
  "orderbook": 1
}'
</textarea> 
          </div> 
         </div> 
        </div>

        <div class="docs-box" id="api_cancel_a_bid"> 
         <h2> <strong>Cancel a Bid</strong> </h2> 
         <div class="docs-box-body"> 
          <p> Schedules a Bid for cancelation as soon as our Matching Engine unlocks it. It sets the order status to "To be cancelled (3)" immediately, and then you can check your <a href="#orders">Orders</a> to see when it's actually cancelled. </p> 
          <strong>URL</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <span class="method">POST</span> 
           <span class="url">https://bitex.la/api-v1/rest/<em>private/bids/<strong>bid_id</strong>/cancel</em></span> 
          </div> 
          <strong>JSON Request</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <span><pre class="highlight"><code><span class="p">{</span><span class="nt">"api_key"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"your_api_key"</span><span class="p">}</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Your bitex.la API key</span><span class="w"> </span></code></pre> </span> 
          </div> 
          <strong>JSON Response</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <span><pre class="highlight"><code><span class="p">[</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// 1 means it's a Bid, see our API class reference.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">12345678</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Bid's unique ID</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">946685400</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Creation time as UNIX timestamp</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Orderbook (1 is BTC/USD)</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mf">100.00000000</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Amount you wanted to spend initially.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mf">10.00000000</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Remaining Amount to be spent.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mf">1000.00000000</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Price: Maximum price you're willing to pay per unit.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">3</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Always 3, meaning the order was scheduled for cancelation.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Always 0, since it has not been cancelled yet.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mf">1.1</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Base currency amount (ie: BTC amount) produced by</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// this Bid (so far). A sum of all the Base currency</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// received on Buy Transactions. Fees are already</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// deducted from this amount.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"ApiKey#1"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Bid issuer. If the order was entered via API it</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// will be an ApiKey, if it was entered via the web</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// UI it will be a User. May be empty for older orders.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mf">0.01</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Amount of Specie paid as fee (so far).</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// A sum of all the fees paid on Buy Transactions.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">]</span><span class="w"> </span></code></pre> </span> 
          </div> 
          <strong>cURL example pastebox</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <textarea class="pastebox" rows="3">curl -X POST https://bitex.la/api-v1/rest/private/bids/&lt;bid_id&gt;/cancel -H "Content-Type: application/json" -d '{
  "api_key": "your_api_key"
}'
</textarea> 
          </div> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="docs-box" id="api_create_an_ask_sell_order"> 
         <h2> <strong>Create an Ask (Sell Order)</strong> </h2> 
         <div class="docs-box-body"> 
          <p> Places a new sell limit order for the amount of Specie specified and charging the specified price or more. Returns a list representing the newly created Ask. </p> 
          <p> Asks are executed until all the Specie amount is sold or until you cancel them. If someone was buying above your price you'll end up getting more USD than anticipated. </p> 
          <p> All Asks are accepted in the 'Received (1)' state, and are moved into the 'Executing (2)' state by our trading engine once it checks your available Specie sufices to place the order, only then your Ask becomes eligible to be matched. You can check this order status in your list of <a href="#orders">Orders</a> </p> 
          <strong>URL</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <span class="method">POST</span> 
           <span class="url">https://bitex.la/api-v1/rest/<em>private/asks</em></span> 
          </div> 
          <strong>JSON Request</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <span><pre class="highlight"><code><span class="p">{</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"api_key"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"your_api_key"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">//Your Bitex.la API key.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"amount"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"10.00"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">//Amount of base currency (ie: BTC) to sell. Must be at least 0.005.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"price"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"500.00"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">//Minimum price you're willing to charge per unit.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"orderbook"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">//Orderbook ID. Optional. Defaults to 1 which is BTC/USD</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">}</span><span class="w"> </span></code></pre> </span> 
          </div> 
          <strong>JSON Response</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <span><pre class="highlight"><code><span class="p">[</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">2</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// 2 means it's an Ask, see our API class reference.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">12345678</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Ask's unique ID</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">946685400</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Creation time as UNIX timestamp</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Orderbook (1 is BTC/USD)</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mf">100.00000000</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Amount you wanted to sell initially.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mf">10.00000000</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Remaining Amount to be sold.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mf">1000.00000000</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Price: Minimum price you're asking for each unit.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Always 1, meaning the order was received and</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// queued to check if you have enough funds.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Always 0, since this order has not been cancelled.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mf">200.0</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// USD produced by this ask (so far). A sum of all</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// the USD received on Sale Transactions. Fees are</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// already deducted from this amount.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"ApiKey#1"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Ask issuer. If the order was entered via API it</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// will be an ApiKey, if it was entered via the web</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// UI it will be a User. May be empty for older orders.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mf">0.1</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Amount of USD paid as fee (so far).</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// A sum of all the fees paid on Sale Transactions.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">]</span><span class="w"> </span></code></pre> </span> 
          </div> 
          <strong>cURL example pastebox</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <textarea class="pastebox" rows="6">curl -X POST https://bitex.la/api-v1/rest/private/asks -H "Content-Type: application/json" -d '{
  "api_key": "your_api_key",
  "amount": "10.00",
  "price": "500.00",
  "orderbook": 1
}'
</textarea> 
          </div> 
         </div>

        <div class="docs-box" id="api_cancel_an_ask"> 
         <h2> <strong>Cancel an Ask</strong> </h2> 
         <div class="docs-box-body"> 
          <p> Schedules an Ask for cancelation as soon as our Matching Engine unlocks it. It sets the order status to "To be cancelled (3)" immediately, and then you can check your <a href="Orders">#orders</a> to see when it's actually cancelled. </p> 
          <p> Returns the Ask with the new "To be cancelled (3)" status, notice your order may still be in use by our engine, so the Remaining amount may change between the time you request the cancelation and the order is really cancelled. </p> 
          <strong>URL</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <span class="method">POST</span> 
           <span class="url">https://bitex.la/api-v1/rest/<em>private/asks/<strong>ask_id</strong>/cancel</em></span> 
          </div> 
          <strong>JSON Request</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <span><pre class="highlight"><code><span class="p">{</span><span class="nt">"api_key"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"your_api_key"</span><span class="p">}</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Your bitex.la API key</span><span class="w"> </span></code></pre> </span> 
          </div> 
          <strong>JSON Response</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <span><pre class="highlight"><code><span class="p">[</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">2</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// 2 means it's an Ask, see our API class reference.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">12345678</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Ask's unique ID</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">946685400</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Creation time as UNIX timestamp</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Orderbook (1 is BTC/USD)</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mf">100.00000000</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Amount you wanted to sell initially.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mf">10.00000000</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Remaining Amount to be sold.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mf">1000.00000000</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Price: Minimum price you're asking for each unit.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">3</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Always 3, meaning the order was scheduled for cancelation.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Always 0, since it has not been cancelled yet.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mf">200.0</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// USD produced by this ask (so far). A sum of all</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// the USD received on Sale Transactions.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Fees are already deducted from this amount.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"ApiKey#1"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Ask issuer. If the order was entered via API it</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// will be an ApiKey, if it was entered via the web</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// UI it will be a User. May be empty for older orders.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mf">0.1</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Amount of USD paid as fee (so far).</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// A sum of all the fees paid on Sale Transactions.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">]</span><span class="w"> </span></code></pre> </span> 
          </div> 
          <strong>cURL example pastebox</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <textarea class="pastebox" rows="3">curl -X POST https://bitex.la/api-v1/rest/private/asks/&lt;ask_id&gt;/cancel -H "Content-Type: application/json" -d '{
  "api_key": "your_api_key"
}'
</textarea> 
          </div> 
         </div>
