        <h1 id="trading-bots">Hosted Trading Bots</h1> 
        <p> Trading Bots can manage a Bitcoin sale or buy to help you get a better pricing than you would get if you executed the full amount in a single order. <br> <br> The strategy used by bots is rather simple: They split up the amount to buy or sell in chunks of a given size and place orders at the best market price. <br> <br> Orders are spaced by time_to_live seconds to allow for new buyers and sellers to replenish the orderbook before executing again. Orders will be cancelled after time_to_live seconds if still executing. <br> <br> Bots also make sure to prevent executing in low-liquidity conditions: they will not place new orders if the spread between the best Bid and the best Ask is over 10 USD. </p> 
        <p class="text-danger"> Bots do not check or lock funds! If your robot fails to place an order because of insufficient funds or other, then it will be terminated prematurely. You'll find the termination reason in exit_status. </p> 
        <div class="docs-box" id="api_list_your_buying_bots"> 
         <h2> <strong>List your Buying Bots</strong> </h2> 
         <div class="docs-box-body"> 
          <p> List all bots created in the past 24 hours, newest first. Limited at 200 items. </p> 
          <strong>URL</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <span class="method">GET</span> 
           <span class="url">https://bitex.la/api-v1/rest/<em>private/buying_bots</em></span> 
          </div> 
          <strong>JSON Request</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <span><pre class="highlight"><code><span class="p">{</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"api_key"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"your_api_key"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Your Bitex.la API key.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"full"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"true"</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Include bots older than 24 hours. Results will still be limited to 200 items.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">}</span><span class="w"> </span></code></pre> </span> 
          </div> 
          <strong>JSON Response</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <span><pre class="highlight"><code><span class="p">[</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">{</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"id"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Bitex id for this Bot.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"created_at"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">946685400</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Creation time as UNIX timestamp.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"updated_at"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">946685400</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Last change time as UNIX timestamp.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"user_id"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// This is you.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"orderbook_id"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Orderbook ID. Defaults to 1 which is BTC/USD</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"amount"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mf">1000.00</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Amount to spend buying.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"produced_amount"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mf">0.0</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Bitcoin amount produced by this bot.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"remaining_amount"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mf">1000.00</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Amount remaining to be spent.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"chunk_size"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mf">1.0</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Size in which to split Amount.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"time_to_live"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">20</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// How long to wait for each order to execute, in seconds.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"executing"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="kc">true</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Wether this bot is still running. A bot may stop executing due to one of several reasons, available in exit_status. Bots may have executed partially.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"to_cancel"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="kc">false</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Wether this robot is scheduled to be cancelled as soon as any outstanding orders are cancelled.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"exit_status"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="kc">null</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// The reason for termination of this bot (when not executing).</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// "completed" The full amount was spent buying.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// "cancelled" The order was cancelled per your request.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// "cant_afford_order" An order could not be placed due to insufficient funds.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// "order_was_invalid" Order could not be placed for unexpected reasons.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"issuer_type"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"ApiKey"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Bots may be created explicitly by you, or implicitly when processing payments.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// "User" A User created this bot through our Web UI.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// "ApiKey" Someone created this bot using our API.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// "Payment" This bot was created to settle an incoming payment.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// "CoinDeposit" This order was created following an incoming Bitcoin deposit</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"issuer_id"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// ID of the specific issuer for this bot, ie: Which ApiKey</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">}</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">]</span><span class="w"> </span></code></pre> </span> 
          </div> 
          <strong>cURL example pastebox</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <textarea class="pastebox" rows="4">curl -X GET https://bitex.la/api-v1/rest/private/buying_bots -H "Content-Type: application/json" -d '{
  "api_key": "your_api_key",
  "full": "true"
}'
</textarea> 
          </div> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="docs-box" id="api_create_a_buying_bot"> 
         <h2> <strong>Create a Buying Bot</strong> </h2> 
         <div class="docs-box-body"> 
          <p> Create a new Buying Bot to spend a given amount, split in orders no bigger than chunk_size, waiting time_to_live seconds between orders. </p> 
          <strong>URL</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <span class="method">POST</span> 
           <span class="url">https://bitex.la/api-v1/rest/<em>private/buying_bots</em></span> 
          </div> 
          <strong>JSON Request</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <span><pre class="highlight"><code><span class="p">{</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"api_key"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"your_api_key"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Your Bitex.la API key.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"amount"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mf">10000.05</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Amount of USD to spend. Must be at least 1 USD.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"chunk_size"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mf">500.00</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Split the amount in chunks this big. The reminder, if any will be executed last. Must be at least 1.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"time_to_live"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">20</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Seconds to wait for an order to execute before placing a new one. The robot will still wait before placing a new order, even if the previous one completes before time_to_live. Must be an integer between 10 and 600.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">}</span><span class="w"> </span></code></pre> </span> 
          </div> 
          <strong>JSON Response</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <span><pre class="highlight"><code><span class="p">{</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"id"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Bitex id for this Bot.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"created_at"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">946685400</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Creation time as UNIX timestamp.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"updated_at"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">946685400</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Last change time as UNIX timestamp.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"user_id"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// This is you.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"orderbook_id"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Orderbook ID. Defaults to 1 which is BTC/USD</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"amount"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mf">1000.00</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Amount to spend buying.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"produced_amount"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mf">0.0</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Bitcoin amount produced by this bot.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"remaining_amount"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mf">1000.00</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Amount remaining to be spent.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"chunk_size"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mf">1.0</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Size in which to split Amount.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"time_to_live"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">20</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// How long to wait for each order to execute, in seconds.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"executing"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="kc">true</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Wether this bot is still running. A bot may stop executing due to one of several reasons, available in exit_status. Bots may have executed partially.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"to_cancel"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="kc">false</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Wether this robot is scheduled to be cancelled as soon as any outstanding orders are cancelled.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"exit_status"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="kc">null</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// The reason for termination of this bot (when not executing).</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// "completed" The full amount was spent buying.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// "cancelled" The order was cancelled per your request.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// "cant_afford_order" An order could not be placed due to insufficient funds.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// "order_was_invalid" Order could not be placed for unexpected reasons.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"issuer_type"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"ApiKey"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Bots may be created explicitly by you, or implicitly when processing payments.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// "User" A User created this bot through our Web UI.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// "ApiKey" Someone created this bot using our API.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// "Payment" This bot was created to settle an incoming payment.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// "CoinDeposit" This order was created following an incoming Bitcoin deposit</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"issuer_id"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// ID of the specific issuer for this bot, ie: Which ApiKey</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">}</span><span class="w"> </span></code></pre> </span> 
          </div>

  "api_key": "your_api_key",
  "amount": 10000.05,

        <div class="docs-box" id="api_create_a_selling_bot"> 
         <h2> <strong>Create a Selling Bot</strong> </h2> 
         <div class="docs-box-body"> 
          <p> Create a new Selling Bot to sell a given amount, split in orders no bigger than chunk_size, waiting time_to_live seconds between orders. </p> 
          <strong>URL</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <span class="method">POST</span> 
           <span class="url">https://bitex.la/api-v1/rest/<em>private/selling_bots</em></span> 
          </div> 
          <strong>JSON Request</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <span><pre class="highlight"><code><span class="p">{</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"api_key"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"your_api_key"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Your Bitex.la API key.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"amount"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mf">10.0000</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Amount of BTC to sell. Must be at least 0.005 BTC.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"chunk_size"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mf">1.00</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Split the amount in chunks this big. The reminder, if any will be executed last. Must be at least 0.005.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"time_to_live"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">20</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Seconds to wait for an order to execute before placing a new one. The robot will still wait before placing a new order, even if the previous one completes before time_to_live. Must be an integer between 10 and 600.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">}</span><span class="w"> </span></code></pre> </span> 
          </div> 
          <strong>JSON Response</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <span><pre class="highlight"><code><span class="p">{</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"id"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Bitex id for this Bot.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"created_at"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">946685400</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Creation time as UNIX timestamp.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"updated_at"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">946685400</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Last change time as UNIX timestamp.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"user_id"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// This is you.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"orderbook_id"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Orderbook ID. Defaults to 1 which is BTC/USD</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"amount"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mf">10.0000</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Amount to sell.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"produced_amount"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mf">200.0</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Bitcoin amount produced by this bot.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"remaining_amount"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mf">10.00</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Amount remaining to be spent.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"chunk_size"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mf">1.0</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Size in which to split Amount.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"time_to_live"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">20</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// How long to wait for each order to execute, in seconds.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"executing"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="kc">true</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Wether this bot is still running. A bot may stop executing due to one of several reasons, available in exit_status. Bots may have executed partially.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"to_cancel"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="kc">false</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Wether this robot is scheduled to be cancelled as soon as any outstanding orders are cancelled.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"exit_status"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="kc">null</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// The reason for termination of this bot (when not executing).</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// "completed" The full amount was spent buying.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// "cancelled" The order was cancelled per your request.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// "cant_afford_order" An order could not be placed due to insufficient funds.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// "order_was_invalid" Order could not be placed for unexpected reasons.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"issuer_type"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"ApiKey"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Bots may be created explicitly by you, or implicitly when processing payments.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// "User" A User created this bot through our Web UI.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// "ApiKey" Someone created this bot using our API.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// "Payment" This bot was created to settle an incoming payment.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// "CoinDeposit" This order was created following an incoming Bitcoin deposit</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"issuer_id"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// ID of the specific issuer for this bot, ie: Which ApiKey</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">}</span><span class="w"> </span></code></pre> </span> 
          </div> 
          <strong>cURL example pastebox</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <textarea class="pastebox" rows="6">curl -X POST https://bitex.la/api-v1/rest/private/selling_bots -H "Content-Type: application/json" -d '{
  "api_key": "your_api_key",
  "amount": 10.0,
  "chunk_size": 1.0,
  "time_to_live": 20
}'
</textarea> 
          </div> 
         </div> 
        </div>

        <h1 id="funding-usd">Deposit &amp; Withdraw USD</h1> 
        <p> You can fund your Bitex account via international wire transfer or local wire transfer where available. </p> 
        <p> Transfered funds will be converted to USD by our bank at their own rate, which is not controlled by us. </p> 
        <p> All deposits and withdrawals should be to someone with an accepted <a href="#kyc-profiles">KYC Profile</a> in this account. </p> 
        <p> Deposits done via international bank transfer need to be announced using this endpoints. </p> 
        <div class="docs-box" id="api_create_a_usd_deposit"> 
         <h2> <strong>Create a USD Deposit</strong> </h2> 
         <div class="docs-box-body"> 
          <p> Announces your intent of depositing cash into your account, which is a required step for some funding options like international bank transfers. </p> 
          <p> When funding via bank transfer you need to tell us the source and amount, so that we can instruct our bank to receive the transfer, due to compliance concerns we may not accept bank transfers that have not been announced by the sender. You should use the request_details to provide sender's name, country, as well as the bank name and country. </p> 
          <p> All Deposits are accepted in the 'Pending (1)' state, and are moved into the 'Accepted (2)' or 'Rejected (3)' state when processed by our account officials. </p> 
          <strong>URL</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <span class="method">POST</span> 
           <span class="url">https://bitex.la/api-v1/rest/<em>private/usd/deposits</em></span> 
          </div> 
          <strong>JSON Request</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <span><pre class="highlight"><code><span class="p">{</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"api_key"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"your_api_key"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Your Bitex.la API key.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"country"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"UY"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// ISO country code of country of origin.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"amount"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mf">100.00</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Amount to deposit, expressed in currency.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"currency"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"UYU"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// ISO currency code, should match country unless we state otherwise.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"deposit_method"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"bank"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">//</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"request_details"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"SWIFT: 899889..."</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Free form field for adding source bank account information or any other message to our account officers.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"kyc_profile_id"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Optional: Unique ID for the KYC Profile sending this deposit, defaults to your main KYC Profile.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">}</span><span class="w"> </span></code></pre> </span> 
          </div> 
          <strong>JSON Response</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <span><pre class="highlight"><code><span class="p">[</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">7</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// It's a USD Deposit, see our API class reference.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">12345678</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Deposit id</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">946685400</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Creation time as UNIX timestamp</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mf">100.00000000</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Intended amount, for customer pre-announced deposits.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mf">100.00000000</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Actual amount credited.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">3</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// An integer representing the used deposit method:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// 2 - Wire Transfer / Other</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// 3 - MoreMT (deprecated)</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Status, always 1 meaning we're waiting for funds to credit</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Always 0, since it has not been cancelled.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"UY"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Country of origin for this deposit. Possible values are AR, BR, CL, CO, PE, UY, MX and US</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"UYU"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Currency in which the Intended amount was expressed. Possible values are ARS, BRL, CLP, COP, PEN, UYU, MXN and USD. Check our rates API for cash_in currency conversion rates</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Kyc Profile ID for which this deposit was instructed.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"Bank of ..."</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Extra information about this deposit set by the user.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"{link:"</span><span class="c1">...</span><span class="s2">"}"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// (Deprecated) AstroPay response body, for astropay deposits only. It's a JSON containing a 'link' attribute which is AstroPay's payment page for this deposit.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"ABCDABCDEAB"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Id of this deposit as set by the payment processor if any.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">3</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Id of the actual currency credited on bitex, as you may deposit local currency but it ends up credited as USD. '3' means you'll get United States Dollars. We may enable balances in other currencies in the future.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">]</span><span class="w"> </span></code></pre> </span> 
          </div>

  "api_key": "your_api_key",
  "country": "UY",
  "amount": 100.0,
  "currency": "UYU",
  "deposit_method": "bank",
  "request_details": "SWIFT: 899889...",
  "kyc_profile_id": 1
}'

        <div class="docs-box" id="api_cancel_a_usd_deposit"> 
         <h2> <strong>Cancel a USD Deposit</strong> </h2> 
         <div class="docs-box-body"> 
          <p> Cancels a pending cash deposit, if you changed your mind about it. Beware you should not cancel a deposit if you have already paid and you're just waiting for it to be confirmed by us. If a deposit does not credit to your account contact us before cancelling it. </p> 
          <strong>URL</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <span class="method">POST</span> 
           <span class="url">https://bitex.la/api-v1/rest/<em>private/usd/deposits/<strong>deposit_id</strong>/cancel</em></span> 
          </div> 
          <strong>JSON Request</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <span><pre class="highlight"><code><span class="p">{</span><span class="nt">"api_key"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"your_api_key"</span><span class="p">}</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Your bitex.la API key</span><span class="w"> </span></code></pre> </span> 
          </div> 
          <strong>JSON Response</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <span><pre class="highlight"><code><span class="p">[</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">7</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// It's a USD Deposit, see our API class reference.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">12345678</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Deposit id</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">946685400</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Creation time as UNIX timestamp</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mf">100.00000000</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Intended amount, for customer pre-announced deposits.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mf">100.00000000</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Actual amount credited.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">3</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// An integer representing the used deposit method:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// 2 - Not cancelled.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// 1 - Deposit did not credit, funds never arrived to our account.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// 2 - We could not accept these funds because the sender is unknown to us.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// 3 - Other, we'll contact you regarding this deposit.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// 4 - This deposit was cancelled per your request.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"UY"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Country of origin for this deposit. Possible values are AR, BR, CL, CO, PE, UY, MX and US</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"UYU"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Currency in which the Intended amount was expressed. Possible values are ARS, BRL, CLP, COP, PEN, UYU, MXN and USD. Check our rates API for cash_in currency conversion rates</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Kyc Profile ID for which this deposit was instructed.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"Bank of ..."</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Extra information about this deposit set by the user.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"{link:"</span><span class="c1">...</span><span class="s2">"}"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// (Deprecated) AstroPay response body, for astropay deposits only.         <div class="docs-box" id="api_create_a_usd_withdrawal"> 
         <h2> <strong>Create a USD Withdrawal</strong> </h2> 
         <div class="docs-box-body"> 
          <p> Request a USD withdrawal from your bitex balance. You only need to set the amount and refer us to a previously created Withdrawal Instruction which specifies a domestic or international bank account, beneficiary details, etc. See the <a href="#create-withdrawal-instruction">Withdrawal Instructions</a> endpoints to learn more about them, and the available countries and withdrawal methods. </p> 
          <p> All Withdrawals are accepted in the 'Received (1)' state, and are moved into the 'Pending (2)' state immediately if you have enough funds, then they're moved the 'Accepted (2)' or 'Rejected (3)' state when processed by our account officials. </p> 
          <strong>URL</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <span class="method">POST</span> 
           <span class="url">https://bitex.la/api-v1/rest/<em>private/usd/withdrawals</em></span> 
          </div> 
          <strong>JSON Request</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <span><pre class="highlight"><code><span class="p">{</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"api_key"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"your_api_key"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Your Bitex.la API key.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"amount"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mf">100.00</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Amount to withdraw in USD.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"withdrawal_instruction_id"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Unique ID for the Withdrawal Instruction to use. See the Withdrawal Instructions section for more info.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"kyc_profile_id"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Optional: Unique ID for the KYC Profile receiving this withdrawal, defaults to your main KYC Profile.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">}</span><span class="w"> </span></code></pre> </span> 
          </div> 
          <strong>JSON Response</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <span><pre class="highlight"><code><span class="p">[</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">8</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// It's a USD Withdrawal, see our API class reference</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">12345678</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Withdrawal id</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">946685400</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Creation time as UNIX timestamp.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mf">100.00000000</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Requested withdrawal Amount in USD</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Status, always 1 meaning it was received and our engine is checking if you have enough funds.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Always 0, since it has not been cancelled.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"UY"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Country ouf destination for this withdrawal. Possible values are AR, BR, CL, CO, PE, UY, MX and US.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"UYU"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Currency in which this withdrawal will be paid, Possible values are ARS, BRL, CLP, COP, PEN, UYU, MXN and USD. Check our rates API for cash_out currency conversion rates.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// "bb", - Cash Out method, one of:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// "international_bank" - International bank transfer.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"bb"</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Other payment method, to be arranged with our staff.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"Billy Bob"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// An optional custom label for this withdrawal info</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Kyc Profile ID for which this deposit was instructed.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">{</span><span class="c1">...</span><span class="p">},</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// The Withdrawal Instructions provided for this withdrawal.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">3</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Id of the actual currency debited on bitex, as you may end up receiving local currency from a withdrawal to your USD balance. 3 means you'll be debited United States Dollars. We may enable balances in other currencies in the future.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">]</span><span class="w"> </span></code></pre> </span> 
          </div> 
          <strong>cURL example pastebox</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <textarea class="pastebox" rows="6">curl -X POST https://bitex.la/api-v1/rest/private/usd/withdrawals -H "Content-Type: application/json" -d '{
  "api_key": "your_api_key",
  "amount": 100.0,
  "withdrawal_instruction_id": 1,
  "kyc_profile_id": 1
}'
</textarea> 
          </div> 
         </div>

Received, our engine is checking if you have enough funds, should be quick.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// 2 - Pending, your withdrawal was accepted and is being processed, may take a few hours.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// 3 - Done, your withdrawal was processed.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// 4 - Cancelled, your withdrawal could not be processed, check the 'reason' field"</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// An integer representing the cancellation reason:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// 0 -         <div class="docs-box" id="api_create_a_usd_withdrawal_instruction"> 
         <h2> <strong>Create a USD Withdrawal instruction</strong> </h2> 
         <div class="docs-box-body"> 
          <p> Store a new set of instructions to be used when requesting cash withdrawals from Bitex or other brokers/exchanges in the Bitex Concierge network. </p> 
          <strong>URL</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <span class="method">POST</span> 
           <span class="url">https://bitex.la/api-v1/rest/<em>private/usd/withdrawal_instructions</em></span> 
          </div> 
          <strong>JSON Request</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <span><pre class="highlight"><code><span class="p">{</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"api_key"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"your_api_key"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Your Bitex.la API key.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"body"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">{</span><span class="nt">"..."</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"..."</span><span class="p">},</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// JSON with all the fields required to request a withdrawal from a broker in the concierge network. These may be your domestic or international bank account information. See below for some examples.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"label"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"Some Label"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Optional. For your convenience.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"schema"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"bitex"</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Optional. Defaults to bitex. See the response description for more information.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">}</span><span class="w"> </span></code></pre> </span> 
          </div> 
          <strong>JSON Response</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <span><pre class="highlight"><code><span class="p">{</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"id"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// This withdrawal instruction ID</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"body"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">{</span><span class="c1">...</span><span class="p">},</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// The JSON fields you provided. See below for examples.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"label"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"Some Label"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// This instruction short label</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"schema"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"bitex"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Whose rules to use when validating the</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// provided body. Each broker in the concierge</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// network may offer different withdrawal</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// methods, in different countries, and</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// that means your instruction body should</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// be initialy validated and sanity checked</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// using that broker's rules.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Other possible value is 'base' which is</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// less strict but knows fewer payment methods.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"created_at"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">946685400</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Creation time as UNIX timestamp</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">}</span><span class="w"> </span></code></pre> </span> 
          </div> 
          <strong>cURL example pastebox</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <textarea class="pastebox" rows="8">curl -X POST https://bitex.la/api-v1/rest/private/usd/withdrawal_instructions -H "Content-Type: application/json" -d '{
  "api_key": "your_api_key",
  "body": {
    "...": "..."
  },
  "label": "Some Label",
  "schema": "bitex"
}'
</textarea> 
          </div> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="docs-box" id="api_example_withdraw_to_a_domestic_bank"> 
         <h2> <strong>Example: Withdraw to a Domestic Bank</strong> </h2> 
         <div class="docs-box-body"> 
          <p> Store a new set of instructions to be used when requesting cash withdrawals from Bitex or other brokers/exchanges in the Bitex Concierge network. </p> 
          <strong>JSON </strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <span><pre class="highlight"><code><span class="p">{</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"payment_method"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"domestic_bank"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"country"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"AR"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Bank country. Choices are AR, PY or PE.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"currency"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"ARS"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Which currency to withdraw to. Different choices available for each country. </span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// AR: ARS or USD</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// PE: PEN or USD</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"bank"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"bbva"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Beneficiary bank name.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Abbreviated and normalized, different choices available for each country. </span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// AR: galicia, bbva, santander, itau, icbc, hsbc, patagonia, credicoop, supervielle,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// comafi, citi, macro, hipotecario, columbia, bind, nacion, ciudad, bapro, san_juan,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// santa_cruz, cordoba, santa_fe, entre_rios, la_pampa, neuquen, corrientes,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// santiago_del_estero, tierra_del_fuego, formosa, la_rioja, chaco, banco_de_valores, finansur </span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// PE: credito, continental, nacion, scotia, interbank, mi_banco, trabajo, financiero, bbva_pe</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"name"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"John Doe"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// The account holder name. Must be the same person that owns the source bitex account.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"city"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"Buenos Aires"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// City of residence of the account holder.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"address"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"Evergreen avenue 123 zip 1234"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Home or work postal address for the account holder.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"phone"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"15-555-55-55"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// A contact phone number to reach the account holder.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"cuit"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"111111111"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Tax ID, or other ID used on the given country tax agency. For Argentina this is 11 consecutive digits. no dashes.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"cbu"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">2220000200000000000002</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Bank account ID for transfers across domestic banks. CBU for Argentina, 22 consecutive digits. No dashes, no spaces, leading zeros if needed.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"bank_account_number"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">33433333</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Domestic bank account number. Consecutive digits, no dashes no spaces. Length varies between banks and countries.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"account_type"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"checking"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Choices are: checking and savings</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"extra_fields"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"You can add anything"</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// You can include any extra fields you want, they will be stored but won't be validated</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">}</span><span class="w"> </span></code></pre> </span> 
          </div> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="docs-box" id="api_example_withdraw_from_bitex_via_international_bank_transfer"> 
         <h2> <strong>Example: Withdraw from bitex via international bank transfer</strong> </h2> 
         <div class="docs-box-body"> 
          <p> Bitex.la can issue withdrawals as international bank transfers. </p> 
          <strong>JSON </strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <span><pre class="highlight"><code><span class="p">{</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"payment_method"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"international_bank"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"country"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"AR"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Bank country. Choices are AR, CL, MX, PE, UY, US, ES, PY, CN, CO</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"currency"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"USD"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// For now we're only issuing withdrawals in USD, that may be converted to local currency by the beneficiary bank</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"name"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"John Doe"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Beneficiary name. Must be the same person that owns the source bitex account.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"city"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"Buenos Aires"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Beneficiary city of residence.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"address"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"Evergreen avenue 123 zip 1234"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Beneficiary home or work postal address.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"postal_code"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"cxx-1233"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Optional. Beneficiary postal code.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"phone"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"15-555-55-55"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Beneficiary phone number.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"bank"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"Some Bank"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Full Bank name.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"bank_country"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"US"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Bank country. Free form. Can be a 2 letter country iso code.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"bank_city"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"some city"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// City of the branch where the bank account is registered, or main branch city.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"bank_address"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"Some address 123"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Address of the branch where the bank account is registered, or main branch address.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"bank_postal_code"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"Some postal code"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Postal code of the branch where the bank account is registered, or main branch postal code.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"bank_swift"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"BANKUS66"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Bank SWIFT or other applicable BIC</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"bank_account_number"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"334-33333"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Domestic bank account number.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"account_type"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"checking"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Choices are: checking and savings</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"extra_fields"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"You can add anything"</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// You can include any extra fields you want, they will be stored but won't be validated</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">}</span><span class="w"> </span></code></pre> </span> 
          </div> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="docs-box" id="api_example_suggest_a_third_party_for_your_withdrawal"> 
         <h2> <strong>Example: Suggest a third party for your withdrawal</strong> </h2> 
         <div class="docs-box-body"> 
          <p> Bitex.la is open to work with third parties of your choice to issue withdrawals anywhere in the world if possible. We'll contact the beneficiary and work out the details. </p> 
          <strong>JSON </strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <span><pre class="highlight"><code><span class="p">{</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"payment_method"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"third_party"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"country"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"AR"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Where do you want to withdraw. Any country.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"name"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"John Doe"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Name of the person requesting the withdrawal, must be a Bitex.la known customer.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"city"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"Buenos Aires"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// City of residence of the person doing the withdrawal.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"phone"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"15-555-55-55"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// A contact phone number to reach the person requesting the withdrawal.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"extra_fields"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"You can add anything"</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// You can include any extra fields you want, they will be stored but won't be validated</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">}</span><span class="w"> </span></code></pre> </span> 
          </div> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <hr> 
        <h1 id="funding-btc">Deposit &amp; Withdraw BTC</h1> 
        <p> You can deposit bitcoin to your Bitex account by either using your primary deposit address which you can find in your <a href="#profile">Profile</a> Or you can <a href="#create-address">create a new deposit address</a> optionally instructing to have the received bitcoin sold at the best market price upon arrival. </p> 
        <p> Bitcoin deposits in Bitex are credited after 3 confirmations for most cases, but may take up to 6 confirmations in our own node. Each deposit corresponds to a transaction output in the bitcoin network. </p> 
        <p> Bitcoins received using our <a href="#payments-overview">Payments API</a> will ultimately credit in your bitex balance as BTC deposits. Keep in mind a single Payment may be fulfilled by a customer through several individual smaller transactions. </p> 
        <p> Withdrawals are human supervised so they may only be processed during work hours. Let us know if you need an exception. </p> 
        <div class="docs-box" id="api_show_a_btc_deposit"> 
         <h2> <strong>Show a BTC Deposit</strong> </h2> 
         <div class="docs-box-body"> 
          <p> Find a BTC depoist by it's unique Bitex ID. </p> 
          <strong>URL</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <span class="method">POST</span> 
           <span class="url">https://bitex.la/api-v1/rest/<em>private/btc/deposits/<strong>deposit_id</strong></em></span> 
          </div> 
          <strong>JSON Request</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <span><pre class="highlight"><code><span class="p">{</span><span class="nt">"api_key"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"your_api_key"</span><span class="p">}</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Your bitex.la API key</span><span class="w"> </span></code></pre> </span> 
          </div> 
          <strong>JSON Response</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <span><pre class="highlight"><code><span class="p">[</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">5</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// It's a Specie Deposit, see our API class reference</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">12345678</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Deposit id</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">946685400</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Creation time as UNIX timestamp.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Specie (1 for Bitcoin).</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mf">100.00000000</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Amount deposited.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">]</span><span class="w"> </span></code></pre> </span> 
          </div> 
          <strong>cURL example pastebox</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <textarea class="pastebox" rows="3">curl -X POST https://bitex.la/api-v1/rest/private/btc/deposits/&lt;deposit_id&gt; -H "Content-Type: application/json" -d '{
  "api_key": "your_api_key"
}'
</textarea> 
          </div> 
         </div> 
        </div>

           <span><pre class="highlight"><code><span class="p">{</span><span class="nt">"api_key"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"your_api_key"</span><span class="p">}</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Your bitex.la API key</span><span class="w"> </span></code></pre> </span> 
          </div> 
          <strong>JSON Response</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <span><pre class="highlight"><code><span class="p">[</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">[</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">5</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// It's a Specie Deposit, see our API class reference</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">12345678</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Deposit id</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">946685400</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Creation time as UNIX timestamp.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Specie (1 for Bitcoin).</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mf">100.00000000</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Amount deposited.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">]</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">]</span><span class="w"> </span></code></pre> </span> 
          </div> 
          <strong>cURL example pastebox</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <textarea class="pastebox" rows="3">curl -X GET https://bitex.la/api-v1/rest/private/btc/deposits -H "Content-Type: application/json" -d '{
  "api_key": "your_api_key"
}'
</textarea>

        <div class="docs-box" id="api_create_address"> 
         <h2> <strong>Create Address</strong> </h2> 
         <div class="docs-box-body"> 
          <p> Create a new payment address, optionally specifying wheter to automatically sell all bitcoins received with it. </p> 
          <strong>URL</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <span class="method">POST</span> 
           <span class="url">https://bitex.la/api-v1/rest/<em>private/btc/addresses</em></span> 
          </div> 
          <strong>JSON Request</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <span><pre class="highlight"><code><span class="p">{</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"api_key"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"your_api_key"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Your Bitex.la API key.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"auto_sell"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="kc">true</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// If true, a new Selling Bot will be created for the full amount received from each deposit to this address.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">}</span><span class="w"> </span></code></pre> </span> 
          </div> 
          <strong>JSON Response</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <span><pre class="highlight"><code><span class="p">{</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"public_address"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"1ABC..."</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Bitcoin address</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"auto_sell"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="kc">false</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// If true, then a new Selling Bot will be created for each deposit received to this address.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"payment_id"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="kc">null</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// The Payment's ID. If this address was internally issued for a payment.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">}</span><span class="w"> </span></code></pre> </span> 
          </div> 
          <strong>cURL example pastebox</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <textarea class="pastebox" rows="4">curl -X POST https://bitex.la/api-v1/rest/private/btc/addresses -H "Content-Type: application/json" -d '{
  "api_key": "your_api_key",
  "auto_sell": true
}'
</textarea> 
          </div> 
         </div> 
        </div>

           <span><pre class="highlight"><code><span class="p">{</span><span class="nt">"api_key"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"your_api_key"</span><span class="p">}</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Your bitex.la API key</span><span class="w"> </span></code></pre> </span> 
          </div> 
          <strong>JSON Response</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <span><pre class="highlight"><code><span class="p">{</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"public_address"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"1ABC..."</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Bitcoin address</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"auto_sell"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="kc">false</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// If true, then a new Selling Bot will be created for each deposit received to this address.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"payment_id"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="kc">null</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// The Payment's ID. If this address was internally issued for a payment.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">}</span><span class="w"> </span></code></pre> </span>

        <div class="docs-box" id="api_list_addreses"> 
         <h2> <strong>List Addreses</strong> </h2> 
         <div class="docs-box-body"> 
          <p> List all your addresses. This list will include the default addresses created with your bitex account, any new addresses you create via API, and other addresses created for you by bitex internal processes, for example, addresses created for Payments. </p>

          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <span class="method">GET</span> 
           <span class="url">https://bitex.la/api-v1/rest/<em>private/btc/addresses</em></span> 
          </div> 
          <strong>JSON Request</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <span><pre class="highlight"><code><span class="p">{</span><span class="nt">"api_key"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"your_api_key"</span><span class="p">}</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Your bitex.la API key</span><span class="w"> </span></code></pre> </span> 
          </div> 
          <strong>JSON Response</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <span><pre class="highlight"><code><span class="p">[</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">{</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"public_addreses"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"1ABC..."</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Bitcoin address</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"auto_sell"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="kc">false</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// If true, then a new Selling Bot will be created for each deposit received to this address.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"payment_id"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="kc">null</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// The Payment's ID. If this address was internally issued for a payment.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">}</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">]</span><span class="w"> </span></code></pre> </span> 
          </div> 
          <strong>cURL example pastebox</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <textarea class="pastebox" rows="3">curl -X GET https://bitex.la/api-v1/rest/private/btc/addresses -H "Content-Type: application/json" -d '{
  "api_key": "your_api_key"
}'
</textarea> 
          </div> 
         </div>

        <div class="docs-box" id="api_create_a_btc_withdrawal"> 
         <h2> <strong>Create a BTC Withdrawal</strong> </h2> 
         <div class="docs-box-body"> 
          <p> Request a Specie withdrawal to a given address. </p> 
          <p> All Withdrawals are accepted in the 'Received (1)' state, and are moved into the 'Pending (2)' state immediately if you have enough funds, then they're moved the 'Accepted (2)' or 'Rejected (3)' state when processed by our account officials. </p> 
          <strong>URL</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <span class="method">POST</span> 
           <span class="url">https://bitex.la/api-v1/rest/<em>private/btc/withdrawals</em></span> 
          </div> 
          <strong>JSON Request</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <span><pre class="highlight"><code><span class="p">{</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"api_key"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"your_api_key"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Your Bitex.la API key.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"address"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"1abcde..."</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Destination bitcoin address.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"amount"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mf">100.00</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Amount to withdraw.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"label"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"some_label"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Optional: A label for tagging this withdrawal.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"kyc_profile_id"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Optional: Unique ID for the KYC Profile receiving this withdrawal, defaults to your main KYC Profile.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">}</span><span class="w"> </span></code></pre> </span> 
          </div> 
          <strong>JSON Response</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <span><pre class="highlight"><code><span class="p">[</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">6</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// It's a Specie Withdrawal, see our API class reference.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">12345678</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Withdrawal id.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">946685400</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Creation time as UNIX timestamp.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Specie (1 for Bitcoin)</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mf">100.00000000</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Amount withdrawn.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Status, always 1, meaning it was received and our engine is checking if you have enough funds.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Always 0 as it was not cancelled.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"1address.."</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Destination address for this withdrawal.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"my wallet"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// An optional custom label for the destination address.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Kyc Profile ID for which this withdrawal was instructed.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"ABCDEF..."</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Transaction ID, available once it's processed.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">]</span><span class="w"> </span></code></pre> </span> 
          </div> 
          <strong>cURL example pastebox</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <textarea class="pastebox" rows="7">curl -X POST https://bitex.la/api-v1/rest/private/btc/withdrawals -H "Content-Type: application/json" -d '{
  "api_key": "your_api_key",
  "address": "1abcde...",
  "amount": 100.0,
  "label": "some_label",
  "kyc_profile_id": 1
}'
</textarea> 
          </div> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="docs-box" id="api_show_a_btc_withdrawal"> 
         <h2> <strong>Show a BTC Withdrawal</strong> </h2> 
         <div class="docs-box-body"> 
          <p> Find a BTC withdrawal by it's unique Bitex ID. </p> 
          <strong>URL</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <span class="method">GET</span> 
           <span class="url">https://bitex.la/api-v1/rest/<em>private/btc/withdrawals/<strong>deposit_id</strong></em></span> 
          </div> 
          <strong>JSON Request</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <span><pre class="highlight"><code><span class="p">{</span><span class="nt">"api_key"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"your_api_key"</span><span class="p">}</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Your bitex.la API key</span><span class="w"> </span></code></pre> </span> 
          </div> 
          <strong>JSON Response</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <span><pre class="highlight"><code><span class="p">[</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">6</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// It's a Specie Withdrawal, see our API class reference.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">12345678</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Withdrawal id.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">946685400</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Creation time as UNIX timestamp.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Specie (1 for Bitcoin)</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mf">100.00000000</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Amount withdrawn.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// An integer representing this withdrawal status:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// 1 - Received, our engine is checking if you have enough funds, should be quick.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// 2 - Pending, your withdrawal was accepted and is being processed. </span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// This may take a few hours as our staff monitors all withdrawals.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// 3 - Done, your withdrawal was processed and should appear on the network soon.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// 4 - Cancelled, your withdrawal could not be processed, check the 'reason' field.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// An integer representing the cancellation reason</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// 0 - Not cancelled.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// 1 - The instruction was received, but you didn't have enough funds</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// 2 - The destination address was invalid.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"1address.."</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Destination address for this withdrawal.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"my wallet"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// An optional custom label for the destination address.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Kyc Profile ID for which this withdrawal was instructed.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"ABCDEF..."</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">// Transaction ID, available once it's processed.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">]</span><span class="w"> </span></code></pre> </span> 
          </div> 
          <strong>cURL example pastebox</strong> 
          <div class="well well-sm"> 
           <textarea class="pastebox" rows="3">curl -X GET https://bitex.la/api-v1/rest/private/btc/withdrawals/&lt;deposit_id&gt; -H "Content-Type: application/json" -d '{
